## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Setter Called with value] --> B{value is None or isinstance str?}
    B -->|No| C[Assert Error]
    B -->|Yes| D{Current value != new value?}
    D -->|No| E[Return self]
    D -->|Yes| F[Update private attribute]
    F --> G[Call add_dirty_field]
    G --> E
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[is_valid called] --> B{solution_id is str?}
    B -->|No| C[Return False]
    B -->|Yes| D{description is str?}
    D -->|No| C
    D -->|Yes| E{reason_code is str?}
    E -->|No| C
    E -->|Yes| F{name is str?}
    F -->|No| C
    F -->|Yes| G[Return True]
```

stateDiagram-v2

    Initialized --> Valid: All attributes set as strings
    Initialized --> Invalid: Missing or invalid attributes

    Modified --> Valid: is_valid returns True
    Invalid --> Valid: Set all attributes correctly
